${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k}{-{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

lapse derivative:
${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

lapse evolution:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}}{-{{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{tr(K)}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}}$
${ \alpha} _{,t}$ flux term $-{0}$
${ \alpha} _{,t}$ source term ${{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}$

lapse partial evolution
${{ { \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{ { \alpha} _{,k}} _{,t}}$ ; ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ a} _k}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using on lhs only ${{ a} _k} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}$
${{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
subtracting ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}$ from both sides
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}\right)} _{,k}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}}{-{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _k} _{,m}}}} + {{{{ a} _k}} {{tr(b)}}}}\right)}}{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _m} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}} + {{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{tr(K)}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{tr(b)}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$

${{ a} _k} _{,t}$ source term: ${-{{{tr(b)}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}$

metric evolution:
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{ \beta} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ \beta} _j} _{,i}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}}$

symmetrizing ${{ \gamma} _i} _j$

${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,l}} + {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{ b} _i} _j}{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{tr(b)}} \cdot {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{ b} _i} _j}{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}} {{{{ δ} ^r} _k}}}\right)} _{,r}}{-{{{tr(b)}} \cdot {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}$ flux term: $-{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{ b} _i} _j}{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}} {{{{ δ} ^r} _k}}}\right)} _{,r}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}$ source term: ${-{{{tr(b)}} \cdot {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}$

Riemann curvature
${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

Ricci curvature
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{ R} ^k} _i} _k} _j}$
using ${{{{{ R} ^k} _i} _k} _j} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _k} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _j}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _k}}}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _k} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _j}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _j}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _m} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _i}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _i}}\right)}}\right)} _{,j}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _k}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}}}$
cancel terms using symmetries:
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _m} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _i}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _i} _m} _k}}\right)} _{,j}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}}}$
split off terms to rearrange gradient:
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l} _{,k}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p} _{,k}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} + { {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{ {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^p}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}}}$
combining derivatives
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + { {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}}{-{ {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^p}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}}} + {{\left( {-{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}\right)} _{,k}}}$

${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{{ d} _j} _i} ^k} + {{{{ d} _i} _j} ^k}{-{{{2}} {{{{{ d} ^k} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{{ d} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}{-{{{{ d} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}} + {{{{ e} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{{ e} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ d} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{ d} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _m}}} + {{{{ d} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _m}}}{-{{{{ e} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _m}}}}{-{{{{ e} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _m}}}}{-{{{{{{ d} _i} _m} _n}} {{{{{ d} _j} ^m} ^n}}}} + {{{{{{ d} _m} _n} _i}} {{{{{ d} _j} ^m} ^n}}} + {{{{{{ d} _m} _n} _j}} {{{{{ d} _i} ^m} ^n}}}}$

extrinsic curvature evolution:
${{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{ \alpha} _{,i}} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ R} _i} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{ Z} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ Z} _j} _{,i}}}\right)}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{-2}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ Z} _k}}} + {{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{\left({{K}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ K} _i} _k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{ K} _l} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{4}} {{π}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j}} {{\left({{S}{-{\rho}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ S} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}} {{{ \beta} ^k}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _j}} {{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}}}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,i}} _{,j}} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}} _{,k}}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \alpha} _{,j}} _{,k}}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,i}} _{,j}} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{\left( {{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,j}}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}\right)} _{,k}}}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,i}} _{,j}} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{\left( {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}\right)} _{,k}}}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,i}} _{,j}} = {{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
${{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ R} _i} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{ Z} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ Z} _j} _{,i}}}\right)}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{-2}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ Z} _k}}} + {{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{\left({{K}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ K} _i} _k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{ K} _l} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{4}} {{π}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j}} {{\left({{S}{-{\rho}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ S} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}} {{{ \beta} ^k}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _j}} {{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}}}}$
using ${{{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}} {{{ \beta} ^k}}} = {{{\left( {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{ \beta} ^k}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{tr(b)}}}}}$
${{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ R} _i} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{ Z} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ Z} _j} _{,i}}}\right)}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{-2}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ Z} _k}}} + {{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{\left({{K}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ K} _i} _k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{ K} _l} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{4}} {{π}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j}} {{\left({{S}{-{\rho}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ S} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _j}} {{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}}} + {{\left( {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{ \beta} ^k}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{tr(b)}}}}}$
using ${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$
${{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ R} _i} _j}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{ Z} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ Z} _j} _{,i}}}\right)}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{-2}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j}} {{{ Z} _k}}} + {{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{\left({{K}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ K} _i} _k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{ K} _l} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{4}} {{π}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j}} {{\left({{S}{-{\rho}}}\right)}}}{-{{{2}} {{{{ S} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _i}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _j}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{\left( {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{ \beta} ^k}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{tr(b)}}}}}$
using ${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{ Z} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ Z} _j} _{,i}}}\right)}}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{{ Z} _i} _{,k}}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ Z} _j} _{,k}}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}}$
